# How to Boost Your Productivity with AI Tools

> Generative AI tools have made a big impact on business in a short period of time. Many people are using them to make their jobs easier and to help them produce even better work. But it can be hard to know where to begin. Join Dave Birss, innovator and AI expert, as he practically demonstrates how to collaborate with AI tools in the best way. He shares a framework to help you understand how you can

### 1. Your Approach to Using AI in Business

#### The two reasons to use AI in business
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/the-two-reasons-to-use-ai-in-business-29810092?u=76281980)

>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/the-two-reasons-to-use-ai-in-business-29810092?u=76281980&t=0)** - AI can be incredibly helpful in a couple of ways.
>
> **[0:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/the-two-reasons-to-use-ai-in-business-29810092?u=76281980&t=4)** The way that most people use it is to make tasks easier.
>
> **[0:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/the-two-reasons-to-use-ai-in-business-29810092?u=76281980&t=7)** It's great at that, but you can also use it to make you better at what you do, and that I think is far more valuable.
>
> **[0:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/the-two-reasons-to-use-ai-in-business-29810092?u=76281980&t=16)** The way I look at it, some tasks call for excellence, while others are perfectly fine with adequacy.

#### Taking responsibility for the output of AI
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/taking-responsibility-for-the-output-of-ai-29811083?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/taking-responsibility-for-the-output-of-ai-29811083?u=76281980&t=0)** - Now, I can't guarantee that generative AI tools will give you an accurate answer, just as I can't guarantee that Robert in customer services will give an accurate answer.
>
> **[0:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/taking-responsibility-for-the-output-of-ai-29811083?u=76281980&t=10)** Robert, I'm sure this camera that I'm using, he wasn't working properly.
>
> **[0:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/taking-responsibility-for-the-output-of-ai-29811083?u=76281980&t=16)** But who's responsible for the accuracy of the answers you get from an AI assistant?
>
> **[0:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/taking-responsibility-for-the-output-of-ai-29811083?u=76281980&t=21)** I believe it's the person who's using it, which in this case is you.
>
> **[0:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/taking-responsibility-for-the-output-of-ai-29811083?u=76281980&t=27)** That means you shouldn't use anything that AI has generated until you've checked it.
>
> **[0:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/taking-responsibility-for-the-output-of-ai-29811083?u=76281980&t=33)** At the time of filming, generative AIs are rapidly improving, but they still hallucinate, and hallucinate is the term we use for them just making stuff up, which funnily enough is a very human trait.
>
> **[0:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/taking-responsibility-for-the-output-of-ai-29811083?u=76281980&t=47)** You're more likely to get AI hallucinations if you write prompts that don't have sufficient information in them, because the AIs will fill those gaps with information that isn't always true.
>
> **[0:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/taking-responsibility-for-the-output-of-ai-29811083?u=76281980&t=59)** In the case of ChatGPT, it's not currently connected to the internet, as I'm filming this, it's currently using information that's over 18 months out of date.
>
> **[1:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/taking-responsibility-for-the-output-of-ai-29811083?u=76281980&t=69)** Now, this may have changed by the time you watch this video.
>
> **[1:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/taking-responsibility-for-the-output-of-ai-29811083?u=76281980&t=72)** But at the moment, it means that if you ask about something that it doesn't know much about, it might just make up an incorrect answer with complete confidence, just like Robert in customer services.
>
> **[1:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/taking-responsibility-for-the-output-of-ai-29811083?u=76281980&t=84)** And if you ask it for sources to back up its answer, it tends to give you things that look like sources but are in fact entirely fictional.
>
> **[1:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/taking-responsibility-for-the-output-of-ai-29811083?u=76281980&t=94)** We can write prompts that reduce these effects, but we can't guarantee that we're going to eliminate them.
>
> **[1:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/taking-responsibility-for-the-output-of-ai-29811083?u=76281980&t=100)** So remember that AI tools are tools, and that means that the ultimate responsibility is on the person using them.
>
> **[1:48](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/how-to-boost-your-productivity-with-ai-tools-26974255/taking-responsibility-for-the-output-of-ai-29811083?u=76281980&t=108)** So as you experiment with AI, always remember to double-check the information it generates and use your own judgment to ensure accuracy, because any inaccuracies that make it into your work are on you.
